# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# ValidationScheme Type Definition and Methods

## Type Definition

**Location:** `github.com/prometheus/common/model` (v0.67.5)

```go
type ValidationScheme int

const (
	// UnsetValidation represents an undefined ValidationScheme.
	// Should not be used in practice.
	UnsetValidation ValidationScheme = iota

	// LegacyValidation is a setting that requires that all metric and label names
	// conform to the original Prometheus character requirements described by
	// MetricNameRE and LabelNameRE.
	LegacyValidation

	// UTF8Validation only requires that metric and label names be valid UTF-8
	// strings.
	UTF8Validation
)
```

## IsValidMetricName Method

```go
func (s ValidationScheme) IsValidMetricName(metricName string) bool
```

**Returns:** whether `metricName` is valid according to the validation scheme `s`.

- For `LegacyValidation`: Validates against the legacy character requirements (pattern: `^[a-zA-Z_:][a-zA-Z0-9_:]*$`)
- For `UTF8Validation`: Only requires valid UTF-8 encoding

## IsValidLabelName Method

```go
func (s ValidationScheme) IsValidLabelName(labelName string) bool
```

**Returns:** whether `labelName` is valid according to the validation scheme `s`.

- For `LegacyValidation`: Validates against the legacy character requirements (pattern: `^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*$`)
- For `UTF8Validation`: Only requires valid UTF-8 encoding

## Related Configuration

The global default validation scheme is controlled by:
```go
var NameValidationScheme = UTF8Validation
```

This variable determines the global method of name validation used by all calls to deprecated functions like `IsValidMetricName()` and `LabelName.IsValid()`.

# ValidationScheme Type Definition and Methods

## Type Definition

```go
type ValidationScheme int

const (
	UnsetValidation ValidationScheme = iota
	LegacyValidation
	UTF8Validation
)
```

## Key Methods

**String()** - Returns string representation ("unset", "legacy", or "utf8")

**MarshalYAML()** and **UnmarshalYAML()** - Enable YAML serialization/deserialization

**MarshalJSON()** and **UnmarshalJSON()** - Enable JSON serialization/deserialization

**Set(text string)** - Implements pflag.Value interface, accepts empty string, "legacy", or "utf8"

**Type()** - Returns "validationScheme" for pflag compatibility

## Validation Methods

**IsValidMetricName(metricName string) bool** - Validates metric names. For LegacyValidation, checks each rune against legacy requirements. For UTF8Validation, ensures the string is valid UTF-8 and non-empty.

**IsValidLabelName(labelName string) bool** - Similar approach to metric validation. Legacy mode verifies characters are alphanumeric, underscore, or digits (after first position). UTF8 mode requires valid UTF-8 strings only.

Both methods panic if an invalid ValidationScheme is provided.

# ValidationScheme Type and Methods

## Type Definition

```go
type ValidationScheme int

const (
	UnsetValidation ValidationScheme = iota
	LegacyValidation
	UTF8Validation
)
```

## Methods

**String()** - Returns string representation: "unset", "legacy", or "utf8"

**IsValidMetricName(metricName string) bool** - Validates metric names according to the scheme. LegacyValidation checks against character requirements; UTF8Validation ensures "valid UTF-8 strings"

**IsValidLabelName(labelName string) bool** - Validates label names similarly, requiring non-empty strings and scheme-appropriate character validation

**MarshalYAML() (any, error)** - Serializes to YAML format, returning empty string for UnsetValidation or the string representation otherwise

**UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error** - Deserializes from YAML by unmarshaling a string and calling Set()

**Set(text string) error** - Implements pflag.Value interface; accepts empty string (no change), "legacy", or "utf8"

**Type() string** - Returns "validationScheme" for pflag compatibility

**MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error)** - Serializes to JSON as string representation

**UnmarshalJSON(bytes []byte) error** - Deserializes from JSON string and calls Set()

### Type Definition Location
**File:** `/prometheus/common/model/metric.go` (from `github.com/prometheus/common/model` package)

### ValidationScheme Type Definition
```go
type ValidationScheme int

const (
	// UnsetValidation represents an undefined ValidationScheme.
	// Should not be used in practice.
	UnsetValidation ValidationScheme = iota

	// LegacyValidation is a setting that requires that all metric and label names
	// conform to the original Prometheus character requirements described by
	// MetricNameRE and LabelNameRE.
	LegacyValidation

	// UTF8Validation only requires that metric and label names be valid UTF-8
	// strings.
	UTF8Validation
)
```

### Key Method Implementations

**IsValidMetricName(metricName string) bool**
- For `LegacyValidation`: Validates metric names against legacy Prometheus character requirements (pattern: `^[a-zA-Z_:][a-zA-Z0-9_:]*$`)
- For `UTF8Validation`: Only requires valid UTF-8 encoding and non-empty strings
- Panics if ValidationScheme is invalid

**IsValidLabelName(labelName string) bool**
- For `LegacyValidation`: Validates label names against legacy requirements (pattern: `^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*$`)
- For `UTF8Validation`: Only requires valid UTF-8 encoding and non-empty strings
- Panics if ValidationScheme is invalid

### Additional Methods on ValidationScheme
- `String()` - Returns string representation ("unset", "legacy", or "utf8")
- `MarshalYAML() / UnmarshalYAML()` - YAML serialization
- `MarshalJSON() / UnmarshalJSON()` - JSON serialization
- `Set(text string)` - Implement
